\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00514}00514      // I need to add exact pressure, radial velocity and radial velocity}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00515}00515   derivatives here}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00516}00516      // Plus the error from these}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00517}00517      double m=2.*Alpha;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00518}00518      double mu=(1./(sin(m)-\/m*cos(m)));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00519}00519      double exact\_u=(mu/r)*(cos(m*phi)-\/cos(m));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00520}00520      double exact\_p=(2.*mu)*((cos(m*phi)/(r*r))-\/cos(m));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00521}00521      double exact\_dudr=-\/(exact\_u/r);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00522}00522      double exact\_dudphi=-\/mu*m*sin(m*phi)/r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00523}00523 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00524}00524      // If we don't have Stokes flow then we need to overwrite the Stokes}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00525}00525   solution by}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00526}00526      // reading in the correct similarity solution from file}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00527}00527      const double Re = re();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00528}00528      if(Re>1.e-\/8)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00529}00529       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00530}00530        double similarity\_solution,dsimilarity\_solution;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00531}00531        get\_similarity\_solution(theta,Alpha,similarity\_solution,dsimilarity\_solution);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00532}00532        double A = Global\_Physical\_Variables::P2/Alpha;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00533}00533 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00534}00534        exact\_u = similarity\_solution/(r*Alpha);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00535}00535        exact\_p = 2.*(exact\_u/r)-\/(A/(2.*Alpha*Alpha))*((1./(r*r))-\/1.);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00536}00536        exact\_dudr = -\/(exact\_u/r);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00537}00537        exact\_dudphi = dsimilarity\_solution/(r*Alpha);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00538}00538       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00539}00539 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00540}00540      // exact pressure and error}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00541}00541      outfile << exact\_p << "{} "{} << (interpolated\_p\_pnst(s)-\/exact\_p) << "{} "{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00542}00542 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00543}00543      // r and theta for better plotting}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00544}00544      outfile << r << "{} "{} << phi << "{} "{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00545}00545 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00546}00546      // exact and oomph du/dr and du/dphi?}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00547}00547      outfile << exact\_u << "{} "{} << (interpolated\_u\_pnst(s,0)-\/exact\_u) << "{} "{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00548}00548      outfile << exact\_dudr << "{} "{} << (interpolated\_dudx\_pnst(s,0,0)-\/exact\_dudr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00549}00549   << "{} "{}; outfile << exact\_dudphi << "{} "{} <<}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00550}00550   (interpolated\_dudx\_pnst(s,0,1)-\/exact\_dudphi) << "{} "{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00551}00551 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00552}00552      outfile << std::endl;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00553}00553     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00554}00554    outfile << std::endl;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00555}00555   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{polar__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00556}00556   */}
